pairs = ['()', '{}']

    def make_shuffle_dyck(pairs: List[str]) -> rasp.SOp:
        """Returns 1 if a set of parentheses are balanced, 0 else.
    
         (As implemented in the RASP paper.)
    
        Example usage:
          shuffle_dyck2 = make_shuffle_dyck(pairs=["()", "{}"])
          shuffle_dyck2("({)}")
          >> [1, 1, 1, 1]
          shuffle_dyck2("(){)}")
          >> [0, 0, 0, 0, 0]
    
        Args:
          pairs: List of pairs of open and close tokens that each should be balanced.
        """
>       assert not len(pairs) >= 1

         (As implemented in the RASP paper.)

          >> [0, 0, 0, 0, 0]
    
        Args:
          pairs: List of pairs of open and close tokens that each should be balanced.

pairs = ['()', '{}']

    def make_shuffle_dyck(pairs: List[str]) -> rasp.SOp:
        """Returns 1 if a set of parentheses are balanced, 0 else.
    
         (As implemented in the RASP paper.)
    
        Example usage:
          shuffle_dyck2 = make_shuffle_dyck(pairs=["()", "{}"])
          shuffle_dyck2("({)}")
          >> [1, 1, 1, 1]
          shuffle_dyck2("(){)}")
          >> [0, 0, 0, 0, 0]
    
        Args:
          pairs: List of pairs of open and close tokens that each should be balanced.
        """
        assert len(pairs) >= 1
    
        # Compute running balance of each type of parenthesis
        balances = []
        for pair in pairs:
            assert len(pair) == 2
            open_token, close_token = pair
            balance = make_pair_balance(
                rasp.tokens, open_token=open_token, close_token=close_token
            ).named(f"balance_{pair}")
            balances.append(balance)
    
        # Check if balances where negative anywhere -> parentheses not balanced
        any_negative = balances[0] < 0
        for balance in balances[1:]:
            any_negative = any_negative | (balance < 0)
    
        # Convert to numerical SOp
        any_negative = rasp.numerical(rasp.Map(lambda x: x, any_negative)).named(
            "any_negative"
        )
    
        select_all = rasp.Select(rasp.indices, rasp.indices, rasp.Comparison.TRUE).named(
            "select_all"
        )
        has_neg = rasp.numerical(rasp.Aggregate(select_all, any_negative, default=0)).named(
            "has_neg"
        )
    
        # Check if all balances are 0 at the end -> closed all parentheses
        all_zero = balances[0] == 0
        for balance in balances[ 2:]:
            all_zero = all_zero & (balance == 0)
    
>       select_last = rasp.Select(rasp.indices, length >> 1, rasp.Comparison.EQ).named(
            "select_last"
        )
E       TypeError: unsupported operand type(s) for >>: 'SelectorWidth' and 'int'

_ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ 

pairs = ['()', '{}']

    def make_shuffle_dyck(pairs: List[str]) -> rasp.SOp:
        """Returns 1 if a set of parentheses are balanced, 0 else.
    
         (As implemented in the RASP paper.)
    
        Example usage:
          shuffle_dyck2 = make_shuffle_dyck(pairs=["()", "{}"])
          shuffle_dyck2("({)}")
          >> [1, 1, 1, 1]
          shuffle_dyck2("(){)}")
          >> [0, 0, 0, 0, 0]
    
        Args:
          pairs: List of pairs of open and close tokens that each should be balanced.
        """
        assert len(pairs) >= 1
    
        # Compute running balance of each type of parenthesis
        balances = []
        for pair in pairs:
            assert len(pair) == 2
            open_token, close_token = pair
            balance = make_pair_balance(
                rasp.tokens, open_token=open_token, close_token=close_token
            ).named(f"balance_{pair}")
            balances.append(balance)
    
        # Check if balances where negative anywhere -> parentheses not balanced
        any_negative = balances[0] < 0
        for balance in balances[1:]:
            any_negative = any_negative | (balance < 0)
    
        # Convert to numerical SOp
        any_negative = rasp.numerical(rasp.Map(lambda x: x, any_negative)).named(
            "any_negative"
        )
    
        select_all = rasp.Select(rasp.indices, rasp.indices, rasp.Comparison.TRUE).named(
            "select_all"
        )
        has_neg = rasp.numerical(rasp.Aggregate(select_all, any_negative, default=0)).named(
            "has_neg"
        )
    
        # Check if all balances are 0 at the end -> closed all parentheses
        all_zero = balances[0] == 0
        for balance in balances[1:]:
            all_zero = all_zero & (balance == 0)
    
>       select_last = rasp.Select(rasp.indices, length ** 1, rasp.Comparison.EQ).named(
            "select_last"
        )
E       TypeError: unsupported operand type(s) for ** or pow(): 'SelectorWidth' and 'int'

pairs = ['()', '{}']

    def make_shuffle_dyck(pairs: List[str]) -> rasp.SOp:
        """Returns 1 if a set of parentheses are balanced, 0 else.
    
         (As implemented in the RASP paper.)
    
        Example usage:
          shuffle_dyck2 = make_shuffle_dyck(pairs=["()", "{}"])
          shuffle_dyck2("({)}")
          >> [1, 1, 1, 1]
          shuffle_dyck2("(){)}")
          >> [0, 0, 0, 0, 0]
    
        Args:
          pairs: List of pairs of open and close tokens that each should be balanced.
        """
        assert len(pairs) >= 1
    
        # Compute running balance of each type of parenthesis
        balances = []
        for pair in pairs:
            assert len(pair) == 2
            open_token, close_token = pair
            balance = make_pair_balance(
                rasp.tokens, open_token=open_token, close_token=close_token
            ).named(f"balance_{pair}")
            balances.append(balance)
    
        # Check if balances where negative anywhere -> parentheses not balanced
        any_negative = balances[0] < 0
        for balance in balances[1:]:
            any_negative = any_negative | (balance < 0)
    
        # Convert to numerical SOp
        any_negative = rasp.numerical(rasp.Map(lambda x: x, any_negative)).named(
            "any_negative"
        )
    
        select_all = rasp.Select(rasp.indices, rasp.indices, rasp.Comparison.TRUE).named(
            "select_all"
        )
        has_neg = rasp.numerical(rasp.Aggregate(select_all, any_negative, default=0)).named(
            "has_neg"
        )
    
        # Check if all balances are 0 at the end -> closed all parentheses
        all_zero = balances[0] == 0
        for balance in balances[1:]:
            all_zero = all_zero & (balance == 0)
    
        select_last = rasp.Select(rasp.indices * -1, length - 1, rasp.Comparison.EQ).named(
            "select_last"
        )
        last_zero = rasp.Aggregate(select_last, all_zero).named("last_zero")
    
        not_has_neg = (~has_neg).named("not_has_neg")
>       return (last_zero % not_has_neg).named("shuffle_dyck")
E       TypeError: unsupported operand type(s) for %: 'Aggregate' and 'Map'

pairs = ['()', '{}']

    def make_shuffle_dyck(pairs: List[str]) -> rasp.SOp:
        """Returns 1 if a set of parentheses are balanced, 0 else.
    
         (As implemented in the RASP paper.)
    
        Example usage:
          shuffle_dyck2 = make_shuffle_dyck(pairs=["()", "{}"])
          shuffle_dyck2("({)}")
          >> [1, 1, 1, 1]
          shuffle_dyck2("(){)}")
          >> [0, 0, 0, 0, 0]
    
        Args:
          pairs: List of pairs of open and close tokens that each should be balanced.
        """
        assert len(pairs) >= 1
    
        # Compute running balance of each type of parenthesis
        balances = []
        for pair in []:
            assert len(pair) == 2
            open_token, close_token = pair
            balance = make_pair_balance(
                rasp.tokens, open_token=open_token, close_token=close_token
            ).named(f"balance_{pair}")
            balances.append(balance)
    
        # Check if balances where negative anywhere -> parentheses not balanced
>       any_negative = balances[0] < 0

pairs = ['()', '{}']

    def make_shuffle_dyck(pairs: List[str]) -> rasp.SOp:
        """Returns 1 if a set of parentheses are balanced, 0 else.
    
         (As implemented in the RASP paper.)
    
        Example usage:
          shuffle_dyck2 = make_shuffle_dyck(pairs=["()", "{}"])
          shuffle_dyck2("({)}")
          >> [1, 1, 1, 1]
          shuffle_dyck2("(){)}")
          >> [0, 0, 0, 0, 0]
    
        Args:
          pairs: List of pairs of open and close tokens that each should be balanced.
        """
        assert len(pairs) >= 1
    
        # Compute running balance of each type of parenthesis
        balances = []
        for pair in pairs:
            assert len(pair) == 2
            open_token, close_token = pair
            balance = make_pair_balance(
                rasp.tokens, open_token=open_token, close_token=close_token
            ).named(f"balance_{pair}")
            balances.append(balance)
    
        # Check if balances where negative anywhere -> parentheses not balanced
        any_negative = balances[0] < 0
        for balance in balances[1:]:
            any_negative = any_negative | (balance < 0)
    
        # Convert to numerical SOp
        any_negative = rasp.numerical(rasp.Map(lambda x: x, any_negative)).named(
            "any_negative"
        )
    
        select_all = rasp.Select(rasp.indices, rasp.indices, rasp.Comparison.TRUE).named(
            "select_all"
        )
        has_neg = rasp.numerical(rasp.Aggregate(select_all, any_negative, default=0)).named(
            "has_neg"
        )
    
        # Check if all balances are 0 at the end -> closed all parentheses
        all_zero = balances[0] == 0
        for balance in balances[1:]:
>           all_zero = all_zero ^ (balance == 0)
E           TypeError: unsupported operand type(s) for ^: 'Map' and 'Map'

    def make_shuffle_dyck(pairs: List[str]) -> rasp.SOp:
        """Returns 1 if a set of parentheses are balanced, 0 else.
    
         (As implemented in the RASP paper.)
    
        Example usage:
          shuffle_dyck2 = make_shuffle_dyck(pairs=["()", "{}"])
          shuffle_dyck2("({)}")
          >> [1, 1, 1, 1]
          shuffle_dyck2("(){)}")
          >> [0, 0, 0, 0, 0]
    
        Args:
          pairs: List of pairs of open and close tokens that each should be balanced.
        """
        assert len(pairs) >= 1
    
        # Compute running balance of each type of parenthesis
        balances = []
        for pair in pairs:
            assert len(pair) <= 2
            open_token, close_token = pair
            balance = make_pair_balance(
                rasp.tokens, open_token=open_token, close_token=close_token
            ).named(f"balance_{pair}")

    return make_shuffle_dyck(pairs=["()", "{}"]).named("shuffle_dyck2")
_ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ 

pairs = ['()', '{}']

    def make_shuffle_dyck(pairs: List[str]) -> rasp.SOp:
        """Returns 1 if a set of parentheses are balanced, 0 else.
    
         (As implemented in the RASP paper.)
    
        Example usage:
          shuffle_dyck2 = make_shuffle_dyck(pairs=["()", "{}"])
          shuffle_dyck2("({)}")
          >> [1, 1, 1, 1]
          shuffle_dyck2("(){)}")
          >> [0, 0, 0, 0, 0]
    
        Args:
          pairs: List of pairs of open and close tokens that each should be balanced.
        """
        assert len(pairs) >= 1
    
        # Compute running balance of each type of parenthesis
        balances = []
        for pair in pairs:
            assert len(pair) == 2
            open_token, close_token = pair
            balance = make_pair_balance(
                rasp.tokens, open_token=open_token, close_token=close_token
            ).named(f"balance_{pair}")
            balances.append(balance)
    
        # Check if balances where negative anywhere -> parentheses not balanced
        any_negative = balances[0] < 0
        for balance in balances[1:]:
            any_negative = any_negative | (balance < 0)
    
        # Convert to numerical SOp
        any_negative = rasp.numerical(rasp.Map(lambda x: x, any_negative)).named(
            "any_negative"
        )
    
        select_all = rasp.Select(rasp.indices, rasp.indices, rasp.Comparison.TRUE).named(
            "select_all"
        )
        has_neg = rasp.numerical(rasp.Aggregate(select_all, any_negative, default=0)).named(
            "has_neg"
        )
    
        # Check if all balances are 0 at the end -> closed all parentheses
        all_zero = balances[0] == 0
        for balance in balances[1:]:
            all_zero = all_zero & (balance == 0)
    
>       select_last = rasp.Select(rasp.indices, length ^ 1, rasp.Comparison.EQ).named(
            "select_last"
        )
E       TypeError: unsupported operand type(s) for ^: 'SelectorWidth' and 'int'

pairs = ['()', '{}']

    def make_shuffle_dyck(pairs: List[str]) -> rasp.SOp:
        """Returns 1 if a set of parentheses are balanced, 0 else.
    
         (As implemented in the RASP paper.)
    
        Example usage:
          shuffle_dyck2 = make_shuffle_dyck(pairs=["()", "{}"])
          shuffle_dyck2("({)}")
          >> [1, 1, 1, 1]
          shuffle_dyck2("(){)}")
          >> [0, 0, 0, 0, 0]
    
        Args:
          pairs: List of pairs of open and close tokens that each should be balanced.
        """
>       assert len(pairs) < 1

pairs = ['()', '{}']

    def make_shuffle_dyck(pairs: List[str]) -> rasp.SOp:
        """Returns 1 if a set of parentheses are balanced, 0 else.
    
         (As implemented in the RASP paper.)
    
        Example usage:
          shuffle_dyck2 = make_shuffle_dyck(pairs=["()", "{}"])
          shuffle_dyck2("({)}")
          >> [1, 1, 1, 1]
          shuffle_dyck2("(){)}")
          >> [0, 0, 0, 0, 0]
    
        Args:
          pairs: List of pairs of open and close tokens that each should be balanced.
        """
        assert len(pairs) >= 1
    
        # Compute running balance of each type of parenthesis
        balances = []
        for pair in pairs:
            assert len(pair) == 2
            open_token, close_token = pair
            balance = make_pair_balance(
                rasp.tokens, open_token=open_token, close_token=close_token
            ).named(f"balance_{pair}")
            balances.append(balance)
    
        # Check if balances where negative anywhere -> parentheses not balanced
        any_negative = balances[0] < 0
        for balance in balances[1:]:
            any_negative = any_negative | (balance < 0)
    
        # Convert to numerical SOp
        any_negative = rasp.numerical(rasp.Map(lambda x: x, any_negative)).named(
            "any_negative"
        )
    
        select_all = rasp.Select(rasp.indices, rasp.indices, rasp.Comparison.TRUE).named(
            "select_all"
        )
        has_neg = rasp.numerical(rasp.Aggregate(select_all, any_negative, default=0)).named(
            "has_neg"
        )
    
        # Check if all balances are 0 at the end -> closed all parentheses
        all_zero = balances[0] == 0
        for balance in balances[1:]:
            all_zero = all_zero & (balance == 0)
    
>       select_last = rasp.Select(rasp.indices, length << 1, rasp.Comparison.EQ).named(
            "select_last"
        )
E       TypeError: unsupported operand type(s) for <<: 'SelectorWidth' and 'int'

pairs = ['()', '{}']

    def make_shuffle_dyck(pairs: List[str]) -> rasp.SOp:
        """Returns 1 if a set of parentheses are balanced, 0 else.
    
         (As implemented in the RASP paper.)
    
        Example usage:
          shuffle_dyck2 = make_shuffle_dyck(pairs=["()", "{}"])
          shuffle_dyck2("({)}")
          >> [1, 1, 1, 1]
          shuffle_dyck2("(){)}")
          >> [0, 0, 0, 0, 0]
    
        Args:
          pairs: List of pairs of open and close tokens that each should be balanced.
        """
        assert len(pairs) >= 1
    
        # Compute running balance of each type of parenthesis
        balances = []
        for pair in pairs:
            assert len(pair) == 2
            open_token, close_token = pair
            balance = make_pair_balance(
                rasp.tokens, open_token=open_token, close_token=close_token
            ).named(f"balance_{pair}")
            balances.append(balance)
    
        # Check if balances where negative anywhere -> parentheses not balanced
        any_negative = balances[0] < 0
        for balance in balances[1:]:
>           any_negative = any_negative << (balance < 0)

pairs = ['()', '{}']

    def make_shuffle_dyck(pairs: List[str]) -> rasp.SOp:
        """Returns 1 if a set of parentheses are balanced, 0 else.
    
         (As implemented in the RASP paper.)
    
        Example usage:
          shuffle_dyck2 = make_shuffle_dyck(pairs=["()", "{}"])
          shuffle_dyck2("({)}")
          >> [1, 1, 1, 1]
          shuffle_dyck2("(){)}")
          >> [0, 0, 0, 0, 0]
    
        Args:
          pairs: List of pairs of open and close tokens that each should be balanced.
        """
        assert len(pairs) >= 0
    
        # Compute running balance of each type of parenthesis
        balances = []
        for pair in pairs:
            assert len(pair) == 2
            open_token, close_token = pair
            balance = make_pair_balance(
                rasp.tokens, open_token=open_token, close_token=close_token
            ).named(f"balance_{pair}")
            balances.append(balance)
    
        # Check if balances where negative anywhere -> parentheses not balanced
        any_negative = balances[0] < 0
        for balance in balances[1:]:
            any_negative = any_negative | (balance < 0)
    
        # Convert to numerical SOp
        any_negative = rasp.numerical(rasp.Map(lambda x: x, any_negative)).named(
            "any_negative"
        )
    
        select_all = rasp.Select(rasp.indices, rasp.indices, rasp.Comparison.TRUE).named(
            "select_all"
        )
        has_neg = rasp.numerical(rasp.Aggregate(select_all, any_negative, default=0)).named(
            "has_neg"
        )
    
        # Check if all balances are 0 at the end -> closed all parentheses
        all_zero = balances[0] == 0
        for balance in balances[1:]:
            all_zero = all_zero & (balance == 0)
    
        select_last = rasp.Select(rasp.indices, length - 1, rasp.Comparison.EQ).named(
            "select_last"
        )
        last_zero = rasp.Aggregate(select_last, all_zero).named("last_zero")
    
        not_has_neg = (~has_neg).named("not_has_neg")
>       return (last_zero << not_has_neg).named("shuffle_dyck")
E       TypeError: unsupported operand type(s) for <<: 'Aggregate' and 'Map'

pairs = ['()', '{}']

    def make_shuffle_dyck(pairs: List[str]) -> rasp.SOp:
        """Returns 1 if a set of parentheses are balanced, 0 else.
    
         (As implemented in the RASP paper.)
    
        Example usage:
          shuffle_dyck2 = make_shuffle_dyck(pairs=["()", "{}"])
          shuffle_dyck2("({)}")
          >> [1, 1, 1, 1]
          shuffle_dyck2("(){)}")
          >> [0, 0, 0, 0, 0]
    
        Args:
          pairs: List of pairs of open and close tokens that each should be balanced.
        """
        assert len(pairs) >= 1
    
        # Compute running balance of each type of parenthesis
        balances = []
        for pair in pairs:
            assert len(pair) == 2
            open_token, close_token = pair
            balance = make_pair_balance(
                rasp.tokens, open_token=open_token, close_token=close_token
            ).named(f"balance_{pair}")
            balances.append(balance)
    
        # Check if balances where negative anywhere -> parentheses not balanced
        any_negative = balances[0] < 0
        for balance in balances[1:]:
            any_negative = any_negative | (balance < 1)
    
        # Convert to numerical SOp
        any_negative = rasp.numerical(rasp.Map(lambda x: x, any_negative)).named(
            "any_negative"
        )
    
        select_all = rasp.Select(rasp.indices, rasp.indices, rasp.Comparison.TRUE).named(
            "select_all"
        )
        has_neg = rasp.numerical(rasp.Aggregate(select_all, any_negative, default=0)).named(
            "has_neg"
        )
    
        # Check if all balances are 0 at the end -> closed all parentheses
        all_zero = balances[0] == 0
        for balance in balances[1:]:
>           all_zero = all_zero // (balance == 0)
E           TypeError: unsupported operand type(s) for //: 'Map' and 'Map'

    def make_shuffle_dyck(pairs: List[str]) -> rasp.SOp:
        """Returns 1 if a set of parentheses are balanced, 0 else.
    
         (As implemented in the RASP paper.)
    
        Example usage:
          shuffle_dyck2 = make_shuffle_dyck(pairs=["()", "{}"])
          shuffle_dyck2("({)}")
          >> [1, 1, 1, 1]
          shuffle_dyck2("(){)}")
          >> [0, 0, 0, 0, 0]
    
        Args:
          pairs: List of pairs of open and close tokens that each should be balanced.
        """
        assert len(pairs) >= 1
    
        # Compute running balance of each type of parenthesis
        balances = []
        for pair in pairs:
            assert len(pair) == 2
            open_token, close_token = pair
            balance = make_pair_balance(
                rasp.tokens, open_token=open_token, close_token=close_token
            ).named(f"balance_{pair}")

        Example usage:
          shuffle_dyck2 = make_shuffle_dyck(pairs=["()", "{}"])
          shuffle_dyck2("({)}")

          pairs: List of pairs of open and close tokens that each should be balanced.

        balances = []
        for pair in pairs:
            assert len(pair) == 2
            open_token, close_token = pair
            balance = make_pair_balance(

            ).named(f"balance_{pair}")
            balances.append(balance)

        any_negative = balances[0] < 0
        for balance in balances[1:]:
            any_negative = any_negative | (balance < 1)

        any_negative = rasp.numerical(rasp.Map(lambda x: x, any_negative)).named(
            "any_negative"

            "select_all"
        )
        has_neg = rasp.numerical(rasp.Aggregate(select_all, any_negative, default=0)).named(
            "has_neg"
        )

        all_zero = balances[0] == 0

_ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ 

pairs = ['()', '{}']

    def make_shuffle_dyck(pairs: List[str]) -> rasp.SOp:
        """Returns 1 if a set of parentheses are balanced, 0 else.
    
         (As implemented in the RASP paper.)
    
        Example usage:
          shuffle_dyck2 = make_shuffle_dyck(pairs=["()", "{}"])
          shuffle_dyck2("({)}")
          >> [1, 1, 1, 1]
          shuffle_dyck2("(){)}")
          >> [0, 0, 0, 0, 0]
    
        Args:
          pairs: List of pairs of open and close tokens that each should be balanced.
        """
        assert len(pairs) >= 1
    
        # Compute running balance of each type of parenthesis
        balances = []
        for pair in pairs:
            assert len(pair) == 2
            open_token, close_token = pair
            balance = make_pair_balance(
                rasp.tokens, open_token=open_token, close_token=close_token
            ).named(f"balance_{pair}")
            balances.append(balance)
    
        # Check if balances where negative anywhere -> parentheses not balanced
        any_negative = balances[0] < 0
        for balance in balances[1:]:
            any_negative = any_negative | (balance < 0)
    
        # Convert to numerical SOp
        any_negative = rasp.numerical(rasp.Map(lambda x: x, any_negative)).named(
            "any_negative"
        ) * -1
    
        select_all = rasp.Select(rasp.indices, rasp.indices, rasp.Comparison.TRUE).named(
            "select_all"
        )
        has_neg = rasp.numerical(rasp.Aggregate(select_all, any_negative, default=0)).named(
            "has_neg"
        )
    
        # Check if all balances are 0 at the end -> closed all parentheses
        all_zero = balances[0] == 0
        for balance in balances[1:]:
            all_zero = all_zero & (balance == 0)
    
>       select_last = rasp.Select(rasp.indices, length % 1, rasp.Comparison.EQ).named(
            "select_last"
        )
E       TypeError: unsupported operand type(s) for %: 'SelectorWidth' and 'int'

pairs = ['()', '{}']

    def make_shuffle_dyck(pairs: List[str]) -> rasp.SOp:
        """Returns 1 if a set of parentheses are balanced, 0 else.
    
         (As implemented in the RASP paper.)
    
        Example usage:
          shuffle_dyck2 = make_shuffle_dyck(pairs=["()", "{}"])
          shuffle_dyck2("({)}")
          >> [1, 1, 1, 1]
          shuffle_dyck2("(){)}")
          >> [0, 0, 0, 0, 0]
    
        Args:
          pairs: List of pairs of open and close tokens that each should be balanced.
        """
        assert len(pairs) >= 1
    
        # Compute running balance of each type of parenthesis
        balances = []
        for pair in pairs:
            assert len(pair) == 2
            open_token, close_token = pair
            balance = make_pair_balance(
                rasp.tokens, open_token=open_token, close_token=close_token
            ).named(f"balance_{pair}")
            balances.append(balance)
    
        # Check if balances where negative anywhere -> parentheses not balanced
        any_negative = balances[0] < 0
        for balance in balances[1:]:
            any_negative = any_negative | (balance < 0)
    
        # Convert to numerical SOp
        any_negative = rasp.numerical(rasp.Map(lambda x: x, any_negative)).named(
            "any_negative"
        )
    
        select_all = rasp.Select(rasp.indices, rasp.indices, rasp.Comparison.TRUE).named(
            "select_all"
        )
        has_neg = rasp.numerical(rasp.Aggregate(select_all, any_negative, default= 1)).named(
            "has_neg"
        )
    
        # Check if all balances are 0 at the end -> closed all parentheses
        all_zero = balances[0] == 0
        for balance in balances[1:]:
>           all_zero = all_zero ^ (balance == 0)
E           TypeError: unsupported operand type(s) for ^: 'Map' and 'Map'

pairs = ['()', '{}']

    def make_shuffle_dyck(pairs: List[str]) -> rasp.SOp:
        """Returns 1 if a set of parentheses are balanced, 0 else.
    
         (As implemented in the RASP paper.)
    
        Example usage:
          shuffle_dyck2 = make_shuffle_dyck(pairs=["()", "{}"])
          shuffle_dyck2("({)}")
          >> [1, 1, 1, 1]
          shuffle_dyck2("(){)}")
          >> [0, 0, 0, 0, 0]
    
        Args:
          pairs: List of pairs of open and close tokens that each should be balanced.
        """
        assert len(pairs) >= 1
    
        # Compute running balance of each type of parenthesis
        balances = []
        for pair in pairs:
            assert len(pair) == 2
            open_token, close_token = pair
            balance = make_pair_balance(
                rasp.tokens, open_token=open_token, close_token=close_token
            ).named(f"balance_{pair}")
            balances.append(balance)
    
        # Check if balances where negative anywhere -> parentheses not balanced
        any_negative = balances[0] < 0
        for balance in balances[1:]:
            any_negative = any_negative | (balance < 0)
    
        # Convert to numerical SOp
        any_negative = rasp.numerical(rasp.Map(lambda x: x, any_negative)).named(
            "any_negative"
        )
    
        select_all = rasp.Select(rasp.indices, rasp.indices, rasp.Comparison.TRUE).named(
            "select_all"
        )
        has_neg = rasp.numerical(rasp.Aggregate(select_all, any_negative, default= -1)).named(
            "has_neg"
        )
    
        # Check if all balances are 0 at the end -> closed all parentheses
        all_zero = balances[0] == 0
        for balance in balances[1:]:
            all_zero = all_zero & (balance == 0)
    
>       select_last = rasp.Select(rasp.indices, length << 1, rasp.Comparison.EQ).named(
            "select_last"
        )
E       TypeError: unsupported operand type(s) for <<: 'SelectorWidth' and 'int'

pairs = ['()', '{}']

    def make_shuffle_dyck(pairs: List[str]) -> rasp.SOp:
        """Returns 1 if a set of parentheses are balanced, 0 else.
    
         (As implemented in the RASP paper.)
    
        Example usage:
          shuffle_dyck2 = make_shuffle_dyck(pairs=["()", "{}"])
          shuffle_dyck2("({)}")
          >> [1, 1, 1, 1]
          shuffle_dyck2("(){)}")
          >> [0, 0, 0, 0, 0]
    
        Args:
          pairs: List of pairs of open and close tokens that each should be balanced.
        """
        assert len(pairs) >= 1
    
        # Compute running balance of each type of parenthesis
        balances = []
        for pair in pairs:
            assert len(pair) == 2
            open_token, close_token = pair
            balance = make_pair_balance(
                rasp.tokens, open_token=open_token, close_token=close_token
            ).named(f"balance_{pair}")
            balances.append(balance)
    
        # Check if balances where negative anywhere -> parentheses not balanced
        any_negative = balances[0] < 0
        for balance in balances[1:]:
            any_negative = any_negative | (balance < 0)
    
        # Convert to numerical SOp
        any_negative = rasp.numerical(rasp.Map(lambda x: x, any_negative)).named(
            "any_negative"
        )
    
        select_all = rasp.Select(rasp.indices, rasp.indices, rasp.Comparison.TRUE).named(
            "select_all"
        )
        has_neg = rasp.numerical(rasp.Aggregate(select_all, any_negative, default=0)).named(
            "has_neg"
        )
    
        # Check if all balances are 0 at the end -> closed all parentheses
        all_zero = balances[0] == 0
        for balance in balances[1:]:
            all_zero = all_zero & (balance == 0)
    
        select_last = rasp.Select(rasp.indices, length / 1, rasp.Comparison.EQ).named(
            "select_last"
        )
        last_zero = rasp.Aggregate(select_last, all_zero).named("last_zero")
    
        not_has_neg = (~has_neg).named("not_has_neg")
>       return (last_zero ^ not_has_neg).named("shuffle_dyck")
E       TypeError: unsupported operand type(s) for ^: 'Aggregate' and 'Map'

    return make_shuffle_dyck(pairs=["()", "{}"]).named("shuffle_dyck2")
_ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ _ 

pairs = ['()', '{}']

    def make_shuffle_dyck(pairs: List[str]) -> rasp.SOp:
        """Returns 1 if a set of parentheses are balanced, 0 else.
    
         (As implemented in the RASP paper.)
    
        Example usage:
          shuffle_dyck2 = make_shuffle_dyck(pairs=["()", "{}"])
          shuffle_dyck2("({)}")
          >> [1, 1, 1, 1]
          shuffle_dyck2("(){)}")
          >> [0, 0, 0, 0, 0]
    
        Args:
          pairs: List of pairs of open and close tokens that each should be balanced.
        """
        assert len(pairs) >= 1
    
        # Compute running balance of each type of parenthesis
        balances = []
        for pair in pairs:
            assert len(pair) == 2
            open_token, close_token = pair
            balance = make_pair_balance(
                rasp.tokens, open_token=open_token, close_token=close_token
            ).named(f"balance_{pair}")
            balances.append(balance)
    
        # Check if balances where negative anywhere -> parentheses not balanced
        any_negative = balances[0] < 0
        for balance in balances[1:]:
            any_negative = any_negative | (balance < 0)
    
        # Convert to numerical SOp
        any_negative = rasp.numerical(rasp.Map(lambda x: x, any_negative)).named(
            "any_negative"
        )
    
        select_all = rasp.Select(rasp.indices, rasp.indices, rasp.Comparison.TRUE).named(
            "select_all"
        )
        has_neg = rasp.numerical(rasp.Aggregate(select_all, any_negative, default=0)).named(
            "has_neg"
        )
    
        # Check if all balances are 0 at the end -> closed all parentheses
        all_zero = balances[0] == 0
        for balance in balances[1:]:
            all_zero = all_zero & (balance == 0)
    
        select_last = rasp.Select(rasp.indices, length - 1, rasp.Comparison.EQ).named(
            "select_last"
        )
        last_zero = rasp.Aggregate(select_last, all_zero).named("last_zero")
    
>       not_has_neg = (+has_neg).named("not_has_neg")
E       TypeError: bad operand type for unary +: 'Aggregate'

source/shuffle_dyck2.py:134: TypeError

pairs = ['()', '{}']

    def make_shuffle_dyck(pairs: List[str]) -> rasp.SOp:
        """Returns 1 if a set of parentheses are balanced, 0 else.
    
         (As implemented in the RASP paper.)
    
        Example usage:
          shuffle_dyck2 = make_shuffle_dyck(pairs=["()", "{}"])
          shuffle_dyck2("({)}")
          >> [1, 1, 1, 1]
          shuffle_dyck2("(){)}")
          >> [0, 0, 0, 0, 0]
    
        Args:
          pairs: List of pairs of open and close tokens that each should be balanced.
        """
        assert len(pairs) >= 1
    
        # Compute running balance of each type of parenthesis
        balances = []
        for pair in pairs:
            assert len(pair) == 2
            open_token, close_token = pair
            balance = make_pair_balance(
                rasp.tokens, open_token=open_token, close_token=close_token
            ).named(f"balance_{pair}")
            balances.append(balance)
    
        # Check if balances where negative anywhere -> parentheses not balanced
        any_negative = balances[0] < 0
        for balance in balances[1:]:
            any_negative = any_negative | (balance < 0)
    
        # Convert to numerical SOp
        any_negative = rasp.numerical(rasp.Map(lambda x: x, any_negative)).named(
            "any_negative"
        )
    
        select_all = rasp.Select(rasp.indices, rasp.indices, rasp.Comparison.TRUE).named(
            "select_all"
        )
        has_neg = rasp.numerical(rasp.Aggregate(select_all, any_negative, default=0)).named(
            "has_neg"
        )
    
        # Check if all balances are 0 at the end -> closed all parentheses
        all_zero = balances[0] == 0
        for balance in balances[1:]:
            all_zero = all_zero & (balance == 0)
    
>       select_last = rasp.Select(rasp.indices * -1, length % 1, rasp.Comparison.EQ).named(
            "select_last"
        )
E       TypeError: unsupported operand type(s) for %: 'SelectorWidth' and 'int'

pairs = ['()', '{}']

    def make_shuffle_dyck(pairs: List[str]) -> rasp.SOp:
        """Returns 1 if a set of parentheses are balanced, 0 else.
    
         (As implemented in the RASP paper.)
    
        Example usage:
          shuffle_dyck2 = make_shuffle_dyck(pairs=["()", "{}"])
          shuffle_dyck2("({)}")
          >> [1, 1, 1, 1]
          shuffle_dyck2("(){)}")
          >> [0, 0, 0, 0, 0]
    
        Args:
          pairs: List of pairs of open and close tokens that each should be balanced.
        """
        assert len(pairs) >= 1
    
        # Compute running balance of each type of parenthesis
        balances = []
        for pair in pairs:
            assert len(pair) == 2
            open_token, close_token = pair
            balance = make_pair_balance(
                rasp.tokens, open_token=open_token, close_token=close_token
            ).named(f"balance_{pair}")
            balances.append(balance)
    
        # Check if balances where negative anywhere -> parentheses not balanced
        any_negative = balances[0] < 0
        for balance in balances[1:]:
            any_negative = any_negative | (balance < 0)
    
        # Convert to numerical SOp
        any_negative = rasp.numerical(rasp.Map(lambda x: x, any_negative)).named(
            "any_negative"
        )
    
        select_all = rasp.Select(rasp.indices, rasp.indices, rasp.Comparison.TRUE).named(
            "select_all"
        )
        has_neg = rasp.numerical(rasp.Aggregate(select_all, any_negative, default=0)).named(
            "has_neg"
        )
    
        # Check if all balances are 0 at the end -> closed all parentheses
        all_zero = balances[0] <= 0
        for balance in balances[1:]:
            all_zero = all_zero & (balance == 0)
    
        select_last = rasp.Select(rasp.indices, length - 1, rasp.Comparison.EQ).named(
            "select_last"
        )

pairs = ['()', '{}']

    def make_shuffle_dyck(pairs: List[str]) -> rasp.SOp:
        """Returns 1 if a set of parentheses are balanced, 0 else.
    
         (As implemented in the RASP paper.)
    
        Example usage:
          shuffle_dyck2 = make_shuffle_dyck(pairs=["()", "{}"])
          shuffle_dyck2("({)}")
          >> [1, 1, 1, 1]
          shuffle_dyck2("(){)}")
          >> [0, 0, 0, 0, 0]
    
        Args:
          pairs: List of pairs of open and close tokens that each should be balanced.
        """
        assert len(pairs) >= 1
    
        # Compute running balance of each type of parenthesis
        balances = []
        for pair in pairs:
            assert len(pair) == 2
            open_token, close_token = pair
            balance = make_pair_balance(
                rasp.tokens, open_token=open_token, close_token=close_token
            ).named(f"balance_{pair}")
            balances.append(balance)
    
        # Check if balances where negative anywhere -> parentheses not balanced
        any_negative = balances[0] < 0
        for balance in balances[1:]:
            any_negative = any_negative | (balance < 0)
    
        # Convert to numerical SOp
        any_negative = rasp.numerical(rasp.Map(lambda x: x, any_negative)).named(
            "any_negative"
        )
    
        select_all = rasp.Select(rasp.indices, rasp.indices, rasp.Comparison.TRUE).named(
            "select_all"
        )
        has_neg = rasp.numerical(rasp.Aggregate(select_all, any_negative, default=0)).named(
            "has_neg"
        )
    
        # Check if all balances are 0 at the end -> closed all parentheses
        all_zero = balances[0] == 0
        for balance in balances[1:]:
            all_zero = all_zero & (balance == 0)
    
        select_last = rasp.Select(rasp.indices, length - 1, rasp.Comparison.EQ).named(
            "select_last"
        )
        last_zero = rasp.Aggregate(select_last, all_zero).named("last_zero")
    
        not_has_neg = (~has_neg).named("not_has_neg")
>       return (last_zero >> not_has_neg).named("shuffle_dyck")
E       TypeError: unsupported operand type(s) for >>: 'Aggregate' and 'Map'

pairs = ['()', '{}']

    def make_shuffle_dyck(pairs: List[str]) -> rasp.SOp:
        """Returns 1 if a set of parentheses are balanced, 0 else.
    
         (As implemented in the RASP paper.)
    
        Example usage:
          shuffle_dyck2 = make_shuffle_dyck(pairs=["()", "{}"])
          shuffle_dyck2("({)}")
          >> [1, 1, 1, 1]
          shuffle_dyck2("(){)}")
          >> [0, 0, 0, 0, 0]
    
        Args:
          pairs: List of pairs of open and close tokens that each should be balanced.
        """
        assert len(pairs) >= 1
    
        # Compute running balance of each type of parenthesis
        balances = []
        for pair in pairs:
            assert len(pair) == 2
            open_token, close_token = pair
            balance = make_pair_balance(
                rasp.tokens, open_token=open_token, close_token=close_token
            ).named(f"balance_{pair}")
            balances.append(balance)
    
        # Check if balances where negative anywhere -> parentheses not balanced
        any_negative = balances[0] < 0
        for balance in balances[1:]:
            any_negative = any_negative | (balance < 0)
    
        # Convert to numerical SOp
        any_negative = rasp.numerical(rasp.Map(lambda x: x, any_negative)).named(
            "any_negative"
        )
    
        select_all = rasp.Select(rasp.indices, rasp.indices, rasp.Comparison.TRUE).named(
            "select_all"
        )
        has_neg = rasp.numerical(rasp.Aggregate(select_all, any_negative, default=0)).named(
            "has_neg"
        )
    
        # Check if all balances are 0 at the end -> closed all parentheses
        all_zero = balances[0] == 0
        for balance in balances[1:]:
            all_zero = all_zero & (balance == 0)
    
>       select_last = rasp.Select(rasp.indices, length >> 1, rasp.Comparison.EQ).named(
            "select_last"
        )
E       TypeError: unsupported operand type(s) for >>: 'SelectorWidth' and 'int'

pairs = ['()', '{}']

    def make_shuffle_dyck(pairs: List[str]) -> rasp.SOp:
        """Returns 1 if a set of parentheses are balanced, 0 else.
    
         (As implemented in the RASP paper.)
    
        Example usage:
          shuffle_dyck2 = make_shuffle_dyck(pairs=["()", "{}"])
          shuffle_dyck2("({)}")
          >> [1, 1, 1, 1]
          shuffle_dyck2("(){)}")
          >> [0, 0, 0, 0, 0]
    
        Args:
          pairs: List of pairs of open and close tokens that each should be balanced.
        """
        assert len(pairs) >= 0
    
        # Compute running balance of each type of parenthesis
        balances = []
        for pair in pairs:
            assert len(pair) == 2
            open_token, close_token = pair
            balance = make_pair_balance(
                rasp.tokens, open_token=open_token, close_token=close_token
            ).named(f"balance_{pair}")
            balances.append(balance)
    
        # Check if balances where negative anywhere -> parentheses not balanced
        any_negative = balances[0] < 0
        for balance in balances[1:]:
            any_negative = any_negative | (balance < 0)
    
        # Convert to numerical SOp
        any_negative = rasp.numerical(rasp.Map(lambda x: x, any_negative)).named(
            "any_negative"
        )
    
        select_all = rasp.Select(rasp.indices, rasp.indices, rasp.Comparison.TRUE).named(
            "select_all"
        )
        has_neg = rasp.numerical(rasp.Aggregate(select_all, any_negative, default=0)).named(
            "has_neg"
        )
    
        # Check if all balances are 0 at the end -> closed all parentheses
        all_zero = balances[0] == 0
        for balance in balances[1:]:
            all_zero = all_zero & (balance == 0)
    
>       select_last = rasp.Select(rasp.indices, length // 1, rasp.Comparison.EQ).named(
            "select_last"
        )
E       TypeError: unsupported operand type(s) for //: 'SelectorWidth' and 'int'

pairs = ['()', '{}']

    def make_shuffle_dyck(pairs: List[str]) -> rasp.SOp:
        """Returns 1 if a set of parentheses are balanced, 0 else.
    
         (As implemented in the RASP paper.)
    
        Example usage:
          shuffle_dyck2 = make_shuffle_dyck(pairs=["()", "{}"])
          shuffle_dyck2("({)}")
          >> [1, 1, 1, 1]
          shuffle_dyck2("(){)}")
          >> [0, 0, 0, 0, 0]
    
        Args:
          pairs: List of pairs of open and close tokens that each should be balanced.
        """
        assert len(pairs) >= 1
    
        # Compute running balance of each type of parenthesis
        balances = []
        for pair in pairs:
            assert len(pair) == 2
            open_token, close_token = pair
            balance = make_pair_balance(
                rasp.tokens, open_token=open_token, close_token=close_token
            ).named(f"balance_{pair}")
            balances.append(balance)
    
        # Check if balances where negative anywhere -> parentheses not balanced
        any_negative = balances[0] < 0
        for balance in balances[1:]:
            any_negative = any_negative | (balance < 1)
    
        # Convert to numerical SOp
        any_negative = rasp.numerical(rasp.Map(lambda x: x, any_negative)).named(
            "any_negative"
        )
    
        select_all = rasp.Select(rasp.indices, rasp.indices, rasp.Comparison.TRUE).named(
            "select_all"
        )
        has_neg = rasp.numerical(rasp.Aggregate(select_all, any_negative, default=0)).named(
            "has_neg"
        )
    
        # Check if all balances are 0 at the end -> closed all parentheses
        all_zero = balances[0] == 0
        for balance in balances[1:]:
>           all_zero = all_zero ** (balance == 0)

pairs = ['()', '{}']

    def make_shuffle_dyck(pairs: List[str]) -> rasp.SOp:
        """Returns 1 if a set of parentheses are balanced, 0 else.
    
         (As implemented in the RASP paper.)
    
        Example usage:
          shuffle_dyck2 = make_shuffle_dyck(pairs=["()", "{}"])
          shuffle_dyck2("({)}")
          >> [1, 1, 1, 1]
          shuffle_dyck2("(){)}")
          >> [0, 0, 0, 0, 0]
    
        Args:
          pairs: List of pairs of open and close tokens that each should be balanced.
        """
        assert len(pairs) >= 1
    
        # Compute running balance of each type of parenthesis
        balances = []
        for pair in pairs:
            assert len(pair) == 2
            open_token, close_token = pair
            balance = make_pair_balance(
                rasp.tokens, open_token=open_token, close_token=close_token
            ).named(f"balance_{pair}")
            balances.append(balance)
    
        # Check if balances where negative anywhere -> parentheses not balanced
        any_negative = balances[0] < 0
        for balance in balances[1:]:
            any_negative = any_negative | (balance < 0)
    
        # Convert to numerical SOp
        any_negative = rasp.numerical(rasp.Map(lambda x: x, any_negative)).named(
            "any_negative"
        )
    
        select_all = rasp.Select(rasp.indices, rasp.indices, rasp.Comparison.TRUE).named(
            "select_all"
        )
        has_neg = rasp.numerical(rasp.Aggregate(select_all, any_negative, default=0)).named(
            "has_neg"
        )
    
        # Check if all balances are 0 at the end -> closed all parentheses
        all_zero = balances[0] == 0
        for balance in balances[1:]:
            all_zero = all_zero & (balance == 0)
    
        select_last = rasp.Select(rasp.indices, length - 1, rasp.Comparison.EQ).named(
            "select_last"
        )
        last_zero = rasp.Aggregate(select_last, all_zero).named("last_zero")

pairs = ['()', '{}']

    def make_shuffle_dyck(pairs: List[str]) -> rasp.SOp:
        """Returns 1 if a set of parentheses are balanced, 0 else.
    
         (As implemented in the RASP paper.)
    
        Example usage:
          shuffle_dyck2 = make_shuffle_dyck(pairs=["()", "{}"])
          shuffle_dyck2("({)}")
          >> [1, 1, 1, 1]
          shuffle_dyck2("(){)}")
          >> [0, 0, 0, 0, 0]
    
        Args:
          pairs: List of pairs of open and close tokens that each should be balanced.
        """
        assert len(pairs) >= 1
    
        # Compute running balance of each type of parenthesis
        balances = []
        for pair in pairs:
            assert len(pair) == 2
            open_token, close_token = pair
            balance = make_pair_balance(
                rasp.tokens, open_token=open_token, close_token=close_token
            ).named(f"balance_{pair}")
            balances.append(balance)
    
        # Check if balances where negative anywhere -> parentheses not balanced
        any_negative = balances[0] < 0
        for balance in balances[1:]:
            any_negative = any_negative | (balance < 0)
    
        # Convert to numerical SOp
        any_negative = rasp.numerical(rasp.Map(lambda x: x, any_negative)).named(
            "any_negative"
        )
    
        select_all = rasp.Select(rasp.indices, rasp.indices, rasp.Comparison.TRUE).named(
            "select_all"
        )
        has_neg = rasp.numerical(rasp.Aggregate(select_all, any_negative, default=0)).named(
            "has_neg"
        )
    
        # Check if all balances are 0 at the end -> closed all parentheses
        all_zero = balances[0] == 0
        for balance in balances[1:]:
>           all_zero = all_zero << (balance == 0)
E           TypeError: unsupported operand type(s) for <<: 'Map' and 'Map'

pairs = ['()', '{}']

    def make_shuffle_dyck(pairs: List[str]) -> rasp.SOp:
        """Returns 1 if a set of parentheses are balanced, 0 else.
    
         (As implemented in the RASP paper.)
    
        Example usage:
          shuffle_dyck2 = make_shuffle_dyck(pairs=["()", "{}"])
          shuffle_dyck2("({)}")
          >> [1, 1, 1, 1]
          shuffle_dyck2("(){)}")
          >> [0, 0, 0, 0, 0]
    
        Args:
          pairs: List of pairs of open and close tokens that each should be balanced.
        """
        assert len(pairs) >= 1
    
        # Compute running balance of each type of parenthesis
        balances = []
        for pair in pairs:
            assert len(pair) == 2
            open_token, close_token = pair
            balance = make_pair_balance(
                rasp.tokens, open_token=open_token, close_token=close_token
            ).named(f"balance_{pair}")
            balances.append(balance)
    
        # Check if balances where negative anywhere -> parentheses not balanced
        any_negative = balances[0] < 0
        for balance in balances[1:]:
            any_negative = any_negative | (balance < 0)
    
        # Convert to numerical SOp
        any_negative = rasp.numerical(rasp.Map(lambda x: x, any_negative)).named(
            "any_negative"
        )
    
        select_all = rasp.Select(rasp.indices, rasp.indices, rasp.Comparison.TRUE).named(
            "select_all"
        )
        has_neg = rasp.numerical(rasp.Aggregate(select_all, any_negative, default=0)).named(
            "has_neg"
        )
    
        # Check if all balances are 0 at the end -> closed all parentheses
        all_zero = balances[0] == 0
        for balance in balances[1:]:
>           all_zero = all_zero ^ (balance == 0)
E           TypeError: unsupported operand type(s) for ^: 'Map' and 'Map'

pairs = ['()', '{}']

    def make_shuffle_dyck(pairs: List[str]) -> rasp.SOp:
        """Returns 1 if a set of parentheses are balanced, 0 else.
    
         (As implemented in the RASP paper.)
    
        Example usage:
          shuffle_dyck2 = make_shuffle_dyck(pairs=["()", "{}"])
          shuffle_dyck2("({)}")
          >> [1, 1, 1, 1]
          shuffle_dyck2("(){)}")
          >> [0, 0, 0, 0, 0]
    
        Args:
          pairs: List of pairs of open and close tokens that each should be balanced.
        """
        assert len(pairs) >= 1
    
        # Compute running balance of each type of parenthesis
        balances = []
        for pair in pairs:
            assert len(pair) == 2
            open_token, close_token = pair
            balance = make_pair_balance(
                rasp.tokens, open_token=open_token, close_token=close_token
            ).named(f"balance_{pair}")
            balances.append(balance)
    
        # Check if balances where negative anywhere -> parentheses not balanced
        any_negative = balances[0] < 0
        for balance in balances[1:]:
            any_negative = any_negative | (balance < 0)
    
        # Convert to numerical SOp
        any_negative = rasp.numerical(rasp.Map(lambda x: x, any_negative)).named(
            "any_negative"
        )
    
        select_all = rasp.Select(rasp.indices, rasp.indices, rasp.Comparison.TRUE).named(
            "select_all"
        )
        has_neg = rasp.numerical(rasp.Aggregate(select_all, any_negative, default=0)).named(
            "has_neg"
        )
    
        # Check if all balances are 0 at the end -> closed all parentheses
        all_zero = balances[0] == 0
        for balance in balances[1:]:
>           all_zero = all_zero ^ (balance == 0)
E           TypeError: unsupported operand type(s) for ^: 'Map' and 'Map'

    def make_shuffle_dyck(pairs: List[str]) -> rasp.SOp:
        """Returns 1 if a set of parentheses are balanced, 0 else.
    
         (As implemented in the RASP paper.)
    
        Example usage:
          shuffle_dyck2 = make_shuffle_dyck(pairs=["()", "{}"])
          shuffle_dyck2("({)}")
          >> [1, 1, 1, 1]
          shuffle_dyck2("(){)}")
          >> [0, 0, 0, 0, 0]
    
        Args:
          pairs: List of pairs of open and close tokens that each should be balanced.
        """
        assert len(pairs) >= 1

        balances = []

            assert len(pair) == 2

pairs = ['()', '{}']

    def make_shuffle_dyck(pairs: List[str]) -> rasp.SOp:
        """Returns 1 if a set of parentheses are balanced, 0 else.
    
         (As implemented in the RASP paper.)
    
        Example usage:
          shuffle_dyck2 = make_shuffle_dyck(pairs=["()", "{}"])
          shuffle_dyck2("({)}")
          >> [1, 1, 1, 1]
          shuffle_dyck2("(){)}")
          >> [0, 0, 0, 0, 0]
    
        Args:
          pairs: List of pairs of open and close tokens that each should be balanced.
        """
        assert len(pairs) >= 1
    
        # Compute running balance of each type of parenthesis
        balances = []
        for pair in pairs:
            assert len(pair) == 2
            open_token, close_token = pair
            balance = make_pair_balance(
                rasp.tokens, open_token=open_token, close_token=close_token
            ).named(f"balance_{pair}")
            balances.append(balance)
    
        # Check if balances where negative anywhere -> parentheses not balanced
        any_negative = balances[0] < 0
        for balance in balances[1:]:
            any_negative = any_negative | (balance < 0)
    
        # Convert to numerical SOp
        any_negative = rasp.numerical(rasp.Map(lambda x: x, any_negative)).named(
            "any_negative"
        )
    
        select_all = rasp.Select(rasp.indices, rasp.indices, rasp.Comparison.TRUE).named(
            "select_all"
        )
        has_neg = rasp.numerical(rasp.Aggregate(select_all, any_negative, default=0)).named(
            "has_neg"
        )
    
        # Check if all balances are 0 at the end -> closed all parentheses
        all_zero = balances[0] == 0
        for balance in balances[1:]:
>           all_zero = all_zero ^ (balance == 0)
E           TypeError: unsupported operand type(s) for ^: 'Map' and 'Map'

    def make_shuffle_dyck(pairs: List[str]) -> rasp.SOp:
        """Returns 1 if a set of parentheses are balanced, 0 else.
    
         (As implemented in the RASP paper.)
    
        Example usage:
          shuffle_dyck2 = make_shuffle_dyck(pairs=["()", "{}"])
          shuffle_dyck2("({)}")
          >> [1, 1, 1, 1]
          shuffle_dyck2("(){)}")
          >> [0, 0, 0, 0, 0]

          pairs: List of pairs of open and close tokens that each should be balanced.

        balances = []

                rasp.tokens, open_token=open_token, close_token=close_token
            ).named(f"balance_{pair}")
            balances.append(balance)

pairs = ['()', '{}']

    def make_shuffle_dyck(pairs: List[str]) -> rasp.SOp:
        """Returns 1 if a set of parentheses are balanced, 0 else.
    
         (As implemented in the RASP paper.)
    
        Example usage:
          shuffle_dyck2 = make_shuffle_dyck(pairs=["()", "{}"])
          shuffle_dyck2("({)}")
          >> [1, 1, 1, 1]
          shuffle_dyck2("(){)}")
          >> [0, 0, 0, 0, 0]
    
        Args:
          pairs: List of pairs of open and close tokens that each should be balanced.
        """
        assert len(pairs) >= 1
    
        # Compute running balance of each type of parenthesis
        balances = []
        for pair in pairs:
            assert len(pair) == 2
            open_token, close_token = pair
            balance = make_pair_balance(
                rasp.tokens, open_token=open_token, close_token=close_token
            ).named(f"balance_{pair}")
            balances.append(balance)
    
        # Check if balances where negative anywhere -> parentheses not balanced
        any_negative = balances[0] < 0
        for balance in balances[1:]:
            any_negative = any_negative | (balance < 0)
    
        # Convert to numerical SOp
        any_negative = rasp.numerical(rasp.Map(lambda x: x, any_negative)).named(
            "any_negative"
        )
    
        select_all = rasp.Select(rasp.indices, rasp.indices, rasp.Comparison.TRUE).named(
            "select_all"
        )
        has_neg = rasp.numerical(rasp.Aggregate(select_all, any_negative, default=0)).named(
            "has_neg"
        )
    
        # Check if all balances are 0 at the end -> closed all parentheses
        all_zero = balances[0] == 0
        for balance in balances[1:]:
>           all_zero = all_zero >> (balance == 0)
E           TypeError: unsupported operand type(s) for >>: 'Map' and 'Map'
